8. $\displaystyle \sum_{n=0}^\infty \frac{(-1)^n}{2n+1} \binom{4n}{2n} (2n+1)(-x)^{2n} = \arctan\left(\sqrt{\frac{1+x}{1-x}}\right)$

9. $\displaystyle \int_0^\infty \frac{(1+x^2)^n e^{-x^2/4}}{(1+x^{2n})(1+ix)} dx = \pi^{n+1/2} i^{n} \frac{\Gamma(n+1/2)}{\Gamma(n+1)}$

10. $\displaystyle \int_0^\infty \frac{e^{-x^2/2}}{(1-ix)(1+ix)^3} dx = -\frac{\pi}{8} i$
